<div id="review_646273022" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646273022" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646273022?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646273022" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11808943012751137147"><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14562694525' title='Screenshot_8 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404360265i/10230034.jpg' width='400' height='540' alt='Screenshot_8' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It felt like just yesterday I was reading Beautiful Disaster, yet it felt like it took forever for Beautiful Oblivion to get here...<br/><br/>Cami didn't have a perfect life growing up, in fact she had a pretty shitty one. Working her way through college as a Bartender at the Red Door where she runs into the Maddox boys on a regular basis... but she grew up in this town, knows the reputation of these brothers.<br/><br/>For Trenton Maddox, his family has always been everything. Losing his mother years ago, his f</span>
  <span id="freeText11808943012751137147" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14562694525" title="Screenshot_8 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404360265i/10230034.jpg" width="400" height="540" alt="Screenshot_8" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It felt like just yesterday I was reading Beautiful Disaster, yet it felt like it took forever for Beautiful Oblivion to get here...<br><br>Cami didn't have a perfect life growing up, in fact she had a pretty shitty one. Working her way through college as a Bartender at the Red Door where she runs into the Maddox boys on a regular basis... but she grew up in this town, knows the reputation of these brothers.<br><br>For Trenton Maddox, his family has always been everything. Losing his mother years ago, his father, brothers and he share a bond - a promise to always take care of each other. But there is one thing missing from Trent's life - the girl. <br><br>Trenton begins to pursue Cami under the guise of friendship, but with Cami's absent boyfriend it suddenly turns into more. Suddenly a few hours of interaction while bartending turns into daily visits and Cami starts to ignore the feelings that are growing with each one of those days. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14562694565" title="Screenshot_2 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404360265i/10230035.jpg" width="400" height="501" alt="Screenshot_2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Trenton Maddox wasn't suppose to be the guy you'd fall in love with, fall into bed with - sure, but her heart was suppose to belong to someone else - but that doesn't seem to be the case once she gets to know the real Trent.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14376009230" title="Screenshot_3 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404360265i/10230036.jpg" width="400" height="266" alt="Screenshot_3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let's just begin with a dose of reality... this story mirrored Beautiful Disaster a little, but I loved BD and I think I fell in love with all these boys during the prologue of Walking Disaster so in order for me not to love this would be hard. Then there is the absent boyfriend... cheating is typically a hard limit and the twist in this particular triangle should have made me see red... but again, the fact that T.J. was so absent and not really developed as a character allowed him to stay out of sight out of mind.<br><br>Now on to Trent. Better than Travis, nope. But that is not something that can be accomplished, Travis was just... well... Travis. I loved that he wasn't an asshole (I know, this coming from the girl that loves the asshole), he was persistent and manipulative in the ways he got to spend time with her - and it was adorable. He was swoony and funny all while still holding that flirty streak the Maddox boys are famous for. As for Cami, I liked her and was ready to love her but that twist that I mentioned before, yeah - that kept me from really loving her in the end. <br><br>I did feel like the twist in the plot that comes into play at the end could have been bigger. It wasn't hard to figure out where this story was heading as I found myself focusing on a few things and running through some of the scenarios in my head and solving the mystery pretty early on. The revelation of it all did seem a little flat, but at the same time it really wasn't the focus of this story. <br><br>I think this story will end up in the love it or hate it pile for some. And I can see the points from both sides clearly. But for me, I loved getting a glimpse back into Travis's life through new eyes and I loved the dynamic of BD and was not displeased to see the same formula used with BO. I have a feeling that the future books might change from this format just simply because the other brothers lead a different kind of life than Travis &amp; Trent. I was starting to go cold on this author, needing something to pull me back in and this did it successfully. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11808943012751137147" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/675327441?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer675327441" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9003353527111493709"><b>4.5 I love Maddox Brothers Stars</b><br/><br/><b>If you are expecting Beautiful Disaster 2.0 and a Travis-a-like Hero, then you will be disappointed. With that said, I still enjoyed Beautiful Oblivion VERY MUCH</b><br/><br/>Beautiful Oblivion isn’t like Beautiful Disaster. There’s no “alpha” Hero, no crazy angst or intense storyline, but a sweet, light hearted read about a guarded girl being pursued by a tatted, but lovable boy.<br/><br/>I went into Beautiful Oblivion not knowing anything. All I knew is that it’s a story about one of t</span>
  <span id="freeText9003353527111493709" style="display:none"><b>4.5 I love Maddox Brothers Stars</b><br><br><b>If you are expecting Beautiful Disaster 2.0 and a Travis-a-like Hero, then you will be disappointed. With that said, I still enjoyed Beautiful Oblivion VERY MUCH</b><br><br>Beautiful Oblivion isn’t like Beautiful Disaster. There’s no “alpha” Hero, no crazy angst or intense storyline, but a sweet, light hearted read about a guarded girl being pursued by a tatted, but lovable boy.<br><br>I went into Beautiful Oblivion not knowing anything. All I knew is that it’s a story about one of the Maddox brothers. I like Trenton. No, he’s not like Travis. I find Travis to be a bit irrational and a little bit unstable. So, Trenton is more stable, rational and kind of like a puppy, in the sense, he purses Cami even though Cami has no interests in him and keeps on telling him that.<br><br>Having tats doesn’t make you the “bad” boy I guess.<br><br>Cami was hard for me to like because this book is **GASP** a LOVE TRIANGLE!!! Uggg, you know my thoughts on this.<br><br><b>I.AM.NOT.A.FAN.OF.LOVE.TRIANGLES</b><br><br>I just don’t get them, but I do read them. Cami is in a committed long distance relationship with T.J. T.J. is too busy to keep up with the relationship, but he’s a REALLY NICE GUY. Another pet peeve of mine is when both of the guys are GREAT! You kind of want to scream at Cami during many parts and question why she’s still with T.J even though they hardly see or speak to each other.<br><br>To each their own I guess.<br><br>Then at some point of the book, Cami “kinda” explains why she doesn’t want to be with Trenton, but we don’t know why until the end.<br><br><b>WHEN YOU FIND OUT, YOUR MIND WILL BE BLOWN</b><br><br>I’m still debating if this is a good or bad thing, but it’s definitely a thing.<br><br>Beautiful Oblivion is a decent read and mostly it’s about Trenton being okay with having a “friendship” with Cami. You will root for Trenton and want to slap Cami. Despite my frustration with Cami, the read is very adorable and sweet.<br><br>There’s no angst and everything is very tamed. It’s almost as if you are reading a book that isn’t written by Jamie McGuire. I’m not sure if I’m okay or disappointed in that. I kind of like it when authors change up their writing style, but I did love the crazy intense story of Beautiful Disaster.<br><br>Regardless, if you are expecting another Beautiful Disaster, you won’t get it, BUT Beautiful Oblivion is still a good read, it just has high expectations attached to it.<br><br><b>Series Order</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11505797.Beautiful_Disaster__Beautiful___1_" title="Beautiful Disaster (Beautiful, #1) by Jamie McGuire" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1358259032s/11505797.jpg" alt="Beautiful Disaster (Beautiful, #1) by Jamie McGuire" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15745950.Walking_Disaster__Beautiful___2_" title="Walking Disaster (Beautiful, #2) by Jamie McGuire" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1352338368s/15745950.jpg" alt="Walking Disaster (Beautiful, #2) by Jamie McGuire" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467165603" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B008J2AH7C/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B008J2AH7C&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=G4MTVJSBQYCAMGMH" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18104607.Beautiful_Oblivion__Beautiful___3_" title="Beautiful Oblivion (Beautiful, #3) by Jamie McGuire" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1398284779s/18104607.jpg" alt="Beautiful Oblivion (Beautiful, #3) by Jamie McGuire" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <span id="freeText8810688558528591702" style="display:none"><b>Update: July 8, 2013<br>GOOD GOD!!!! FINALLY!</b><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.com/i/5sm8pg" rel="nofollow noopener">

I DON'T WANT to give it a 1 star... I don't want to be annoyed by this... I don't want to be offended by this... But here we are a year later after my initial shock and surprise of getting more of Maddox brothers... we get THIS.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406680740ra/10583512.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It is a great story... if you remove the potholes... and I'm sorry you 3/4/5 stars givers - you are deluding yourself into thinking there aren't HUGE potholes in the story. Most of events and incidences don't make any sense. You can justify it that it's a YA/NA book and it's the story about self discovery and growth... UMMMM NO! it is not. I loved Beautiful Disaster from messed up Trav to naive Pidge AND at least they stayed stable their characters. They were well formed along with support cast that just MADE SENSE.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406680576ra/10583476.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I do not want to go any further into spoiling details for those that still want to take this journey (if you want to PM me and I can vent and maybe you can talk me off the ledge).<br><br>There are certain events that happen in this book that make absolutely no sense and even though this one has a great twist to the story line... there is absolutely nothing that corroborates the twist... If being vague and again full of story potholes corroborating the twist... ummm sure it supported it. <br><br>I'm sorry... but not for me and perhaps I will rethink this rating further... but I can not give it more even if it means I burn some bridges. S'il la vie.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406680820ra/10583518.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_645994092" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/645994092" />
    <a title="Sara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10747133-sara"><img alt="Sara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468189168p2/10747133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/645994092?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara" href="/user/show/10747133-sara">Sara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer645994092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10040932222203350827">So, although I liked this book and didn't want to put it down, I just didn't love it. There wasn't a <b>wow</b> moment, or a time when i was swooning over Trent. I liked him though, he's a Maddox for crying out loud. This also takes place during the time Travis meets Abby, so he does have cameo!<br/>Cami and Trent have grown up together since grade school. Cami is very well aware of the Maddox boys. The fighting and the long line of girls. But she has her own boyfriend, TJ. That's never around. We get a cou</span>
  <span id="freeText10040932222203350827" style="display:none">So, although I liked this book and didn't want to put it down, I just didn't love it. There wasn't a <b>wow</b> moment, or a time when i was swooning over Trent. I liked him though, he's a Maddox for crying out loud. This also takes place during the time Travis meets Abby, so he does have cameo!<br>Cami and Trent have grown up together since grade school. Cami is very well aware of the Maddox boys. The fighting and the long line of girls. But she has her own boyfriend, TJ. That's never around. We get a couple phone calls, texts, a couple of really short visits. He lives in California, and she isn't allowed to tell anyone who he is, that they are dating, or what he does for a living. Hell she doesnt even reallly know what he does. It's a huge cloud of <b>what the fuck</b>. As he's away, she gets closer to Trent.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404077599ra/10188307.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is very low on the angst, pretty much non existent. Even though this is in Cami's POV, I had no doubt how Trent felt about her. He wanted her and he was going to do whatever it took to get her. Boyfriend be damned. And that's what he does. And TJ, he kind of is in the background...<br><br>There really wasn't much cat and mouse with these two. She holds on to her secret tight. Her roommate's boy drama was a part of the story line and at times was more interesting than Cami. Cami's brothers seemed like a bunch a meat-heads though. I mean, for 4 brothers you would think they would want to protect their sister, but they were the complete opposite. It's hard to give details because that would be spoilers... For those wondering the level of "hotness". Its low. Really low. For the Maddox brothers being great with the ladies, you dont really get a taste of that. There is one scene, kinda fade to black sex. Trent is more sugary sweet, although he does get into a couple fights, which was more of a turn on. He's not as rough around the edges as Travis was, and I admit I missed that trait.<br><br>I also felt there was a lot of outside crap interfering in their story. Her parents drama. The douche bag brothers. Reagan's drama (although entertaining). Her two jobs and that drama. If there was less outside crap, maybe they could have had more time for sexytimes, or dating,just something..I also think the book missed the mark in portraying the unattainable Maddox boys. Hell, Trent wasn't running from Cami! He was chasing after her!<br><br>The ending? Well, it was a bummer for me. I guessed early on her secret, and I secretly hoped I was wrong. That there would be another curve ball thrown in. But there wasn't. Sadly. It was revealed and the story was over. Just like that. Reveal, THE END...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404242930ra/10213158.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> Like I said, bummer. Because I had a lot of questions that are unanswered and if the next books are about the other brothers, guess I wont get my answer<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[....but maybe its coming in Thomas's <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10040932222203350827" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1032467550" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1032467550" />
    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1032467550?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy | Foxy Blogs by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer">Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=library2go">library2go</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=headphones">headphones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2014-books">2014-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=august-2014">august-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1032467550" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16424000746110105763"><br/>I've been contemplating how I feel about this book and what I should rate it. <br/><b> <br/>I didn't love it. <br/>Not even sure if I liked most of it.<br/>But I do know I didn't hate it. </b> <br/><br/>And that's where my problem comes in...I'm not sure how I feel about this book. One thing is for sure Ms. McGuire has an addicting writing style that makes it hard to put her books down. <br/><br/>A couple months ago I requested my local online library buy this book for their collection. Most books I've recommended for the library to buy NEVE</span>
  <span id="freeText16424000746110105763" style="display:none"><br>I've been contemplating how I feel about this book and what I should rate it. <br><b> <br>I didn't love it. <br>Not even sure if I liked most of it.<br>But I do know I didn't hate it. </b> <br><br>And that's where my problem comes in...I'm not sure how I feel about this book. One thing is for sure Ms. McGuire has an addicting writing style that makes it hard to put her books down. <br><br>A couple months ago I requested my local online library buy this book for their collection. Most books I've recommended for the library to buy NEVER make the cut. So imagine my surprise Tuesday night when I got an email letting me know that this book was ready for me to pick up. I got an even bigger surprise when I found out that it was an audio book because I'm a fan of audio books. <br><br>The moment I saw this cover I fell in love with it. The vibrant colors of a peacock feathers are eye catching and the name got me too.<b>BEAUTIFUL OBLIVION</b>! To be oblivious, is that beautiful? <b>Sometimes it is</b> if you can just go about you life without distractions. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408598796i/10871827._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Trent</b> and I were both<b> oblivious</b> to<b> Cami's</b> "secret". Maybe if I hadn't been listening to this one I would have picked up on it sooner but I have to say when it was revealed I was so frustrated by the lack of COMMUNICATION that I wanted to throw something. I don't get why that "secret" couldn't be revealed. Maybe as the series goes on I'll understand why it was such a big deal that it was kept from everyone. I'm still left with some questions: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>Why if TJ knew his brother was in love with Cami did he date her in the first place?<br>Why not tell Trent the "big" secret, in the first place?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The drama with Cami's roommate love life was something I didn't care about. I really just wanted to hear about Trent and Cami along with the glimpses of Abby and Travis we got to see. The <b>storyline</b> parallels Beautiful Disaster's book. <br><br>I've been very tempted to re-listen to this one before it has to go back to the library to see if I'd feel differently knowing what I know or *if* I'd still be frustrated by the lack of communication and drama. I guess the extra drama with the roommate and her love triangle was something I could of used less of. <br><br>After some thought I'm going to mark this one <b>3.5 stars</b> because I did enjoy some of it but the drama was over the top at times and most of it could have been eliminated had Cami just shared her secret.<blockquote>
  <b>“Anything to do with the Maddoxes is never boring.” </b>
</blockquote><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18104607.Beautiful_Oblivion__Beautiful___3_" title="Beautiful Oblivion (Beautiful, #3) by Jamie McGuire" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1398284779s/18104607.jpg" alt="Beautiful Oblivion (Beautiful, #3) by Jamie McGuire" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Goodreads has this listed as book #3 of the Beautiful series<b> BUT </b> Amazon and Jamie McGuire have it listed as <b>The Maddox Brothers series (book #1)</b>. <br>The Maddox Brothers will be four novels chronicling the exciting, romantic, and sometimes volatile road to love for the Maddox brothers. To find out when book 2 will be released <a href="http://www.jamiemcguire.com/upcoming-projects/" rel="nofollow noopener">click here.</a><br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408724793i/10887518.png" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=perfect-book-boyfriend">perfect-book-boyfriend</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer748600121" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer852635611716682073"> <b>4 Oblivious Stars</b>	<br/><br/>The younger sister of four brothers Cami never had a easy life. Their brothers are the only thing that makes sense in her life and although they are fiercely protective she is strong and independent… and slightly broken. <br/>Working at The Red Door and again having a weekend canceled with her boyfriend she ends up creating a friendship with Trent Maddox and used to be around men she believes that’s what they’ll always be: friends. <br/>Until Trent falls in love and you know what happen</span>
  <span id="freeText852635611716682073" style="display:none"> <b>4 Oblivious Stars</b>	<br><br>The younger sister of four brothers Cami never had a easy life. Their brothers are the only thing that makes sense in her life and although they are fiercely protective she is strong and independent… and slightly broken. <br>Working at The Red Door and again having a weekend canceled with her boyfriend she ends up creating a friendship with Trent Maddox and used to be around men she believes that’s what they’ll always be: friends. <br>Until Trent falls in love and you know what happens when a Maddox boy falls in love. It’s relentless and it’s forever. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384280184ra/6835476.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Cami has secrets that can jeopardize everything. Big secrets. <br>And when all come clear, could her secret be the only reason why a Maddox boy walks away from the girl he loves? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> A great story with another perfect Maddox boy. I didn’t liked it as much as BD and sometimes it looked like the author was trying to force it to be the awesomeness that BD was, and that’s just not possible. But still, an amazing NA reading that you shouldn’t miss. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person, female POV. Solid and addictive writing. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Cami was a great heroine: strong, fierce and protective. Bonus for not being whinny and annoying. Trent was nearly perfect. I loved him and I dare to say, as much as I loved Travis. He was another perfectly imperfect Maddox boy. And because of that end, I can’t wait to read the book of the next Maddox brother! <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot scenes.<br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_850650634" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/850650634" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/850650634?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer850650634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18419089494955245595"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’ve had a lifetime of wrong. You’re the only thing that’s right.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>I should probably start this review with a small confession—I was not a Beautiful Disaster groupie when everyone was proclaiming their undying love for Travis “Mad Dog” Maddox and naming their daughters Abby. Not because I did not like it, but simply because I never read it when it was first released, and thus never embraced the craze. As curiosity got the better of me and I finally decided to dive in, while I appreci</span>
  <span id="freeText18419089494955245595" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’ve had a lifetime of wrong. You’re the only thing that’s right.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I should probably start this review with a small confession—I was not a Beautiful Disaster groupie when everyone was proclaiming their undying love for Travis “Mad Dog” Maddox and naming their daughters Abby. Not because I did not like it, but simply because I never read it when it was first released, and thus never embraced the craze. As curiosity got the better of me and I finally decided to dive in, while I appreciated why this story was loved so desperately by so many readers out there, I think I was too old to swoon over nineteen-year-old bad boys and obsessive first loves. But I totally got it. I got why this story, this tumultuous type of relationship, appealed to such a wide and varied audience, and how it earned such a loyal cult following by providing the reader with the type of escapism that reminds us all of our first loves, of how impetuous our young hearts once were, and of how crazy and hot-headed that first rush of hormones truly made us. This book, once more, is a reminder of it all, albeit on a more subdued level, but still succeeding in re-awakening the memory of those troublesome years when we were finding ourselves, our place in the world around us, and navigating through life on our own for the very first time, regularly losing ourselves in the oblivion of it all. And all the while adamantly believing that every feeling, every emotion, every mind-blowing ‘first’ was the sum of all we would ever get to experience in life.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“No one has ever wanted someone as much as I want you.”</i>
</blockquote><br>As we return to the delicious world of the Maddox brothers and the young women who steal their hearts at last, we finally get to know Trenton “Trent” Maddox, Travis’ elder brother and the son their widowed father depends on the most. A bad boy of sorts just like his younger brother, Trent’s heavily tattooed façade and hot temper give the impression of walking through life without feeling deeply or becoming emotionally attached to anyone, but nothing could be further from the truth. Beneath this defiant mask hides a sensitive and heartbroken young man whose fear of experiencing loss again, coupled with never having faced his past traumas, have made him a brewing pit of anger and irritability. But just like every fire has a source, every yin has its yang, and Trent’s ‘antidote’ comes in the form of a brown-haired pixie with curves in all the right places and an outspoken personality to match.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“It’s a small town. You shouldn’t have burned all of your bridges.”<br>“There’s a few I haven’t lit a fire under. Yet.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Camille “Cami” Camlin is the girl next door, the oldest child and only girl in a family of all boys, a young woman whose confidence does not stem from the effect she has on the opposite sex, but rather from her self-awareness and determination to be independent in life. And unlike most females of her age, she has remained impervious to the Maddox charm while growing up, and even more so in her early twenties as she has watched them add notch after notch to their headboards. Trent and Cami have known each other all their lives, but were never friends as such. His reputation has always preceded him and thus made him an unwelcome dating candidate in her eyes.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’d seen him flirt, seduce, and evade since we were kids. There was absolutely no trick Trenton Maddox could play that I wouldn’t be ready for.”</i>
</blockquote><br>However, when a Maddox sets his mind on something, he is not to be easily persuaded to change it, and once he enters Cami’s life, Trent is there to stay. Ignoring all her insistent attempts to drive him away and discourage his efforts, he makes himself at home in her daily life, becoming a friend she didn’t know she needed, loyal and protective, all the while not making it secret that he wishes for more. Or that not even Cami’s long distance relationship with a boyfriend she rarely sees would deter him from pursuing her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I was just thinking now was as good a time as any to acknowledge that you’re perfect and it wouldn’t suck if you fell madly in love with me anytime soon.”<br>“I have a boyfriend.”<br>“Speed bump.”</i>
</blockquote><br>The more time they spend with one another, and the more he treats her as if the world revolved around her, the more she starts questioning everything else in her life and facing it all one by one. Trent represents the mess, impulsiveness and uncertainty her past has taught her to fear and avoid at all costs, but he is also the mirror of many qualities she has always wished to eradicate in herself, and the more she allows herself to accept him as he is and all that he embodies, the more she starts accepting those traits in herself, no longer perceiving them as flaws. On the other hand, Cami is a grounding force for Trent’s volatile Maddox gene, his desire to make her love him making him want to be the type of man to deserve her affections. They are opposites in so many ways, and yet when they are together, those differences are what makes them so perfect for one another.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Have you ever wanted something that you knew you shouldn’t have? That it was wrong on every level, but you knew you needed it?”</i>
</blockquote><br>This is in essence a story of two people becoming each other’s passage into adulthood by giving one another the courage to grow up and face their fears. It’s a story that held me enthralled from the very beginning, happy as a clam to indulge in the simplicity of the fantasy of a ‘bad boy’ falling for the ‘good girl’, of a boy pursuing a girl relentlessly, shamelessly and with all his might. I did feel throughout the entire story, however, like I was missing a vital clue, a key of sorts to unlock the motivation behind the heroine’s actions, and I have to admit that until the very last page, she was a paradox to me. But then everything came together all of a sudden, the puzzle pieces all magically falling into place and I found myself speechless, frantically cataloguing the clues we were given unsuspectingly, and finally understanding her character. A few gaps in the story still left me wishing they had been explored and capitalised on more to make it an even more cohesive and emotionally richer storyline, especially references to past events that clearly affected the characters in a way that they now needed to overcome them. But I am hoping that subsequent instalments in this brand new series will fill those gaps and that as we got a new glimpse into Travis and Abby’s story, we will get a similar one into Trent and Cami’s as well.<br><br>This book is an absolute treat for the Beautiful Disaster fans out there, old and new, and one cannot help but fall in love with yet another Maddox brother. It left me greedy for more and with a sudden interest in getting “cashmere comfortable”.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m a f*ckup, but I’m going to get it figured out. I swear. Just . . . don’t give up on me, okay?”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2014/06/21/beautiful-oblivion-jamie-mcguire/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18419089494955245595" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_646144770" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/646144770" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646144770?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=angsty-read">angsty-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646144770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16370570904113375725">*****4.5 STARS*****<br/>(BR with Melissa, Dee, Tiffany, and Sharon)<br/><br/>I had my doubts when I first heard about this book.<br/>After being a bit disappointed with the books that followed <u>"Beautiful Disaster"</u>, I wasn't setting up high expectations for this one.<br/>I was pleasantly surprised at just how much I really loved this book!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/98c0056fe12f777443d79c5ddc2f34f3_zpscf8b64a1.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404786561i/10283308._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 98c0056fe12f777443d79c5ddc2f34f3_zpscf8b64a1.jpg' width='370' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>This story seems to take place during the same time period of "Beautiful Disaster". Cami Camlin works as a bartender at the Red Door, a local bar that the Maddox brothers frequent</span>
  <span id="freeText16370570904113375725" style="display:none">*****4.5 STARS*****<br>(BR with Melissa, Dee, Tiffany, and Sharon)<br><br>I had my doubts when I first heard about this book.<br>After being a bit disappointed with the books that followed <u>"Beautiful Disaster"</u>, I wasn't setting up high expectations for this one.<br>I was pleasantly surprised at just how much I really loved this book!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/98c0056fe12f777443d79c5ddc2f34f3_zpscf8b64a1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404786561i/10283308._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 98c0056fe12f777443d79c5ddc2f34f3_zpscf8b64a1.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This story seems to take place during the same time period of "Beautiful Disaster". Cami Camlin works as a bartender at the Red Door, a local bar that the Maddox brothers frequent. She's known the Maddox brothers since grade school, although she thinks that they don't know that she even exists. She's completely mistaken!!<br>She's also dating a mystery man, named TJ.<br>TJ lives in California and has a job that keeps him away from her most of the time, and is also for whatever reason,so top secret, he can't divulge what he actually does.<br><br><br><br>On a night off, while hanging out at the bar, Trenton decides to make his move. Even though Cami is upfront with him about TJ, Trenton pursues her but plays it off as friendship at first.<br>He is so charming and persistent that eventually Cami finds it pretty hard to deny her feelings that are growing for Trent.<br>I loved little Olive and the relationship Trent had with her. It made him all the more swoonworthy!!<br>It appears as though we have another Maddox brother to fall in love with!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/5f5656c1e2894108f8162cba2dbdd007_zps9eb84bc1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404786561i/10283309._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5f5656c1e2894108f8162cba2dbdd007_zps9eb84bc1.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I never had an issue with Cami.<br>She had a pretty volatile family life due to her alcoholic father and trouble making brothers.<br>She saves up money and moves out on her own to escape that drama but when one of her brothers gets in trouble, she takes on a second job at Second Skin to help him pay off a debt.<br><br><br>This story, to me, was not about cheating or even a love triangle.<br>TJ was barely around and Cami was forthright with TJ and Trent. <br>She did keep a secret for TJ and that was supposed to be the big mystery in the story, but Melissa figured that one right away, and I started to see all the clues pointing to what TJs deal was.<br>He was the person in the wrong in this situation.<br><br><br><br>Cami does realize that Trent is the one she wants to be with and there is some painful angst that will occur around this time!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/e5832ebdc53cb144c66240e762cb299b_zps354f21cc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404786561i/10283310._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e5832ebdc53cb144c66240e762cb299b_zps354f21cc.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I felt like it took forever to get to the sexy times and that maybe we could have had a little more between Cami and Trent, but I wasn't disappointed.<br>I was swept away by how deeply Trent loved Cami and his protectiveness over her.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"Because I've been in love with you since grade school, Chamomile. And everyone knew it. Everyone."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br>I really loved this one but I had to deduct points for the lack of an epilogue, the abrupt ending, and the secret TJ forced Cami to keep, which made no freaking sense to me!!<br> </span>

<div id="review_645949265" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/645949265" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/645949265?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer645949265" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15048345649877767083">3.5 - 4 ★'s <br/><br/>This is the story of Trenton (Trent), Travis' brother, from <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>. He's a tattoo artist trying to do the right things. Cami (Camille) works at a local bar, The Red Door, and just wants to have a normal, happy life. <br/><br/>Let me just start this out by saying there is no way you cannot compare this to <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>. Trenton and Travis are a lot alike so the way they talk, act and go after things are very similar. <br/><br/>Trenton has a mission and her name is Cami. Apparently, he's </span>
  <span id="freeText15048345649877767083" style="display:none">3.5 - 4 ★'s <br><br>This is the story of Trenton (Trent), Travis' brother, from <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>. He's a tattoo artist trying to do the right things. Cami (Camille) works at a local bar, The Red Door, and just wants to have a normal, happy life. <br><br>Let me just start this out by saying there is no way you cannot compare this to <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>. Trenton and Travis are a lot alike so the way they talk, act and go after things are very similar. <br><br>Trenton has a mission and her name is Cami. Apparently, he's been in love with her since they were kids and everyone has known it but her. It's not really clear why he picked now to go after her but there's no stopping him once he decided to. His POV would have made things so much more amazing. <br><br>Cami took a bit for me to warm up to. She's just a bit rough around the edges but once you find out why, it makes you understand her even more. I liked that she was taking charge of her life and she didn't let anyone, even Trent, take that away from her.<br><br>I didn't feel this book was that steamy. There was a lot of sexual tension but when things finally got going, it kind of drizzled out. I almost felt like I missed something. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439876000ra/15897454.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a bit of a twist going on. Cami actually has a boyfriend although he is long distance and basically absent. There's a lot of mystery as to who he is but it's not too hard to figure out. He does cause a lot of problems between Trent and Cami even after Cami breaks up with him. I did love how things came out in the end. <br><br>One of the main problems for me was the lack of emotional intensity. This book's timeline is about the same as <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> and some of those events overshadow this ones. The last 10-15% did provide some much needed drama but unfortunately, it wasn't enough for me.<br><br>We got a lot of other drama though through Cami's roommate, Raegen, and Cami's family. Raegen has some boyfriend issues of her own and Cami's family is just whacked. Her Dad is out of control and all her brother's name start with "C"...it was really confusing to keep them straight except for Coby who has issues of his own. I would have loved to have less of them and more of Trent and Cami.<br><br>However, Olive was one of the best parts of the book! She is the five year old daughter of Trent's neighbor who Trent has taken quite a liking to and her to him. Some of the things that come out of her mouth are sooo adorable! <br><br>Overall, a decent read and I did enjoy it. It would be hard to live up to <i>Beautiful Disaster's</i> success. Hopefully, the next book will be better although I don't have a clue who it will be about! <br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404800481i/10284474.jpg" width="400" height="125" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “I’ve got a bottle of Crown at my apartment and some lunch meat. Let’s drink until we throw up ham sandwiches.”<br><br>♥ “You were pretty comfortable today.” <br><br>“Comfortable? I’m fucking cashmere.”<br><br>♥ “I needed to get my mind off of you.” When I didn’t respond, he turned to me. “I would let a girl rescue me from that torture every night of the week, but even when I was with someone else, all I thought about was you.” <br><br>“That’s not really . . . a compliment,” I said.<br><br>♥ “I <i>am</i> the one, Cami. I’m it for you. I know because you’re it for me.”<br><br>♥ "The first time I saw you on the playground, I knew what beauty was. The first time you ignored me was my first broken heart. I thought I was playing this right, from the moment I sat down at your table at the Red. No one has ever wanted someone as much as I want you."<br><br>♥ “I’m going to marry you someday.” I smiled. <br><br>“When pigs fly.” <br><br>He shrugged. “I can put a pig on a plane. No problem.” <br><br>“Okay, when you dance around in a thong to Britney Spears in front of your dad. That’s when we’ll get married.” <br><br>He took in a long, deep breath, and then blew it out. “Challenge accepted.”<br><br>♥ “I know you don’t believe me, but I really have loved you since we were kids,” he said quietly. “And now I get to love you ’til we’re old.”<br><br><br><br>*BR w/Melissa, Patty, Denisse and Tiffany!*</span>
  <a data-text-id="15048345649877767083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646190900?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646190900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11576268593289825416">***3.5 Stars ***<br/><br/>This is book one in The Maddox Brothers series! Honestly, I was very hopeful that this was going to be another awesome read like “Beautiful Disaster!” Unfortunately, no matter how much I wanted it to be just as good; it fell short for me. One of the biggest factors was the heroine; Cami... I felt she was too closed off in her feelings for Trenton Maddox. There were big reasons why she was stand offish in the beginning... but it got old very fast, and by the time more than half th</span>
  <span id="freeText11576268593289825416" style="display:none">***3.5 Stars ***<br /><br />This is book one in The Maddox Brothers series! Honestly, I was very hopeful that this was going to be another awesome read like “Beautiful Disaster!” Unfortunately, no matter how much I wanted it to be just as good; it fell short for me. One of the biggest factors was the heroine; Cami... I felt she was too closed off in her feelings for Trenton Maddox. There were big reasons why she was stand offish in the beginning... but it got old very fast, and by the time more than half the book was over... I had enough of her indecisiveness.<br /><br />Trenton Maddox was an absolute sweetheart... he really was... but he put up with way too much crap from Cami... in fact, there were times I felt he was kind of whipped when it came to her. He deserved way better. The secret that Cami had didn’t come out to the very end, and it left me scratching my head. I’m still trying to figure it out. I would have never guessed it, and it almost makes me want to go back and reread the book to see where I might have missed clues!!! <br /><br />All in all, this was just an ok read for me. I’m hoping the next Maddox brothers instalment will be way better!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11576268593289825416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SM8O4EoVWWJzGmbwiPSzD8kC3XR6BCq/GXp4q1LpAOA9DqHtiuNjIxjV7zBgzSSAzhiAByhuN3vKjn8dIqEYHg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NrCncglzNXrAOzUp1FuFhbfu38ngaOb/C6X4mzkn/WBDcQh/yYUPO6v0vOk8YhIKsPSCurIC+zvYUf8tSW/lng==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10385542801405833068">Jamie McGuire was born in Tulsa, Oklahoma. She attended Northern Oklahoma College, the University of Central Oklahoma, and Autry Technology Center where she graduated with a degree in Radiography.<br/><br/>Jamie paved the way for the New Adult genre with the international bestseller Beautiful Disaster. Her follow-up novel, Walking Disaster, debuted at #1 on the New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Jou</span>
  <span id="freeText10385542801405833068" style="display:none">Jamie McGuire was born in Tulsa, Oklahoma. She attended Northern Oklahoma College, the University of Central Oklahoma, and Autry Technology Center where she graduated with a degree in Radiography.<br /><br />Jamie paved the way for the New Adult genre with the international bestseller Beautiful Disaster. Her follow-up novel, Walking Disaster, debuted at #1 on the New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestseller lists in all four categories. Beautiful Oblivion, book one of the Maddox Brothers series, also topped the New York Times bestseller list, debuting at #1. In 2015, books two and three of the Maddox Brothers series, Beautiful Redemption and Beautiful Sacrifice, respectively, also topped the New York Times, as well as a Beautiful series novella, Something Beautiful. In 2016, Beautiful Burn made an appearance on the New York Times and USA Today, and was also named iBooks' Romance Book of the Year. The same year, A Beautiful Funeral also topped the New York Times bestseller list.<br /><br />Novels also written by Jamie McGuire include: apocalyptic thriller and 2014 UtopYA Best Dystopian Book of the Year, Red Hill; the Providence series, a young adult paranormal romance trilogy; Apolonia, a dark sci-fi romance; and several novellas, including A Beautiful Wedding, Among Monsters, Happenstance: A Novella Series, and Sins of the Innocent.<br /><br />Jamie is the first indie author in history to strike a print deal with retail giant Wal-Mart. Her self-published novel, Beautiful Redemption hit Wal-Mart shelves in September, 2015.<br /><br />Jamie lives in Steamboat Springs, Colorado with her husband, Jeff, and their three children. <br /><br />Find Jamie at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jamiemcguire.com">www.jamiemcguire.com</a> or on Facebook, Twitter, Google +, and Instagram.</span>
